                        "import wx\n\n# --- Shape Classes ---\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"Base class for all shapes.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start_pos, end_pos, pen=wx.Pen(wx.BLACK, 2), brush=wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 200))):\n        self.start_pos = start_pos\n        self.end_pos = end_pos\n        self.pen = pen\n        self.brush = brush\n        self.selected = False\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Return True if point pt (wx.Point) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move shape by dx, dy.\"\"\"\n        self.start_pos = wx.Point(self.start_pos.x + dx, self.start_pos.y + dy)\n        self.end_pos = wx.Point(self.end_pos.x + dx, self.end_pos.y + dy)\n\n    def get_bounding_box(self):\n        x1, y1 = self.start_pos\n        x2, y2 = self.end_pos\n        left = min(x1, x2)\n        right = max(x1, x2)\n        top = min(y1, y2)\n        bottom = max(y1, y2)\n        return wx.Rect(left, top, right-left, bottom-top)\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        rect = self.get_bounding_box()\n        dc.SetPen(self.pen if not self.selected else wx.Pen(wx.BLUE, 2, wx.PENSTYLE_DOT))\n        dc.SetBrush(self.brush)\n        dc.DrawRectangle(rect)\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        return self.get_bounding_box().Contains(pt)\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        rect = self.get_bounding_box()\n        dc.SetPen(self.pen if not self.selected else wx.Pen(wx.BLUE, 2, wx.PENSTYLE_DOT))\n        dc.SetBrush(self.brush)\n        dc.DrawEllipse(rect)\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        rect = self.get_bounding_box()\n        # Ellipse hit test\n        cx = rect.x + rect.width / 2\n        cy = rect.y + rect.height / 2\n        if rect.width == 0 or rect.height == 0:\n            return False\n        dx = (pt.x - cx) / (rect.width / 2)\n        dy = (pt.y - cy) / (rect.height / 2)\n        return dx*dx + dy*dy <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        dc.SetPen(self.pen if not self.selected else wx.Pen(wx.BLUE, 2, wx.PENSTYLE_DOT))\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start_pos, self.end_pos)\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Hit test: distance from point to line segment\n        x1, y1 = self.start_pos\n        x2, y2 = self.end_pos\n        px, py = pt\n        if x1 == x2 and y1 == y2:\n            return wx.Point(x1, y1).DistanceTo(pt) < 5\n        # Project point onto line segment\n        dx = x2 - x1\n        dy = y2 - y1\n        length_sq = dx*dx + dy*dy\n        t = ((px - x1)*dx + (py - y1)*dy) / length_sq\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        nearest_x = x1 + t*dx\n        nearest_y = y1 + t*dy\n        dist = ((px - nearest_x)**2 + (py - nearest_y)**2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 6  # 6 pixels threshold\n\n# --- Main Drawing Panel ---\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.WHITE)\n        self.shapes = []\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.drawing = False\n        self.dragging = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = wx.Point(0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # Modes: 'select', 'rect', 'ellipse', 'line'\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_motion)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.drawing = False\n        self.dragging = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        dc = wx.BufferedPaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        # Draw all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        # Draw current shape if drawing\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Hit test all shapes, topmost first\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n                if shape.contains(pos):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    self.dragging = True\n                    # Save offset for dragging\n                    bbox = shape.get_bounding_box()\n                    self.drag_offset = wx.Point(pos.x - bbox.x, pos.y - bbox.y)\n                    # Deselect others\n                    for s in self.shapes:\n                        if s != shape:\n                            s.selected = False\n                    self.Refresh()\n                    return\n            # Clicked on empty space: deselect all\n            for s in self.shapes:\n                s.selected = False\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            self.drawing = True\n            if self.mode == 'rect':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape(pos, pos)\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape(pos, pos)\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape(pos, pos)\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.drawing and self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing\n            self.current_shape.end_pos = pos\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            self.drawing = False\n            self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n        elif self.dragging and self.selected_shape:\n            self.dragging = False\n\n    def on_motion(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.drawing and self.current_shape and event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            # Update current shape's end position\n            self.current_shape.end_pos = pos\n            self.Refresh()\n        elif self.dragging and self.selected_shape and event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            # Move selected shape\n            bbox = self.selected_shape.get_bounding_box()\n            new_x = pos.x - self.drag_offset.x\n            new_y = pos.y - self.drag_offset.y\n            dx = new_x - bbox.x\n            dy = new_y - bbox.y\n            self.selected_shape.move(dx, dy)\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        # Right click to deselect\n        for s in self.shapes:\n            s.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n# --- Main Frame with Toolbar ---\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        # Panel for drawing\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n        # Toolbar\n        self.toolbar = self.CreateToolBar()\n        self.add_toolbar_tools()\n        self.toolbar.Realize()\n        # Status bar\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Select a tool to begin.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n\n    def add_toolbar_tools(self):\n        # Add tools for select, rectangle, ellipse, line\n        select_tool = self.toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, 'Select', wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Select/Move\")\n        rect_tool = self.toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, 'Rectangle', wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        ellipse_tool = self.toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, 'Ellipse', wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_HELP_BOOK, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        line_tool = self.toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, 'Line', wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Line\")\n        self.toolbar.AddSeparator()\n        clear_tool = self.toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, 'Clear', wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_DELETE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Clear All\")\n        # Bind events\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.on_tool('select'), select_tool)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.on_tool('rect'), rect_tool)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.on_tool('ellipse'), ellipse_tool)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.on_tool('line'), line_tool)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, self.on_clear, clear_tool)\n\n    def on_tool(self, mode):\n        self.panel.set_mode(mode)\n        tool_names = {'select': 'Selection', 'rect': 'Rectangle', 'ellipse': 'Ellipse', 'line': 'Line'}\n        self.SetStatusText(f\"Mode: {tool_names.get(mode, '')}\")\n\n    def on_clear(self, event):\n        self.panel.shapes.clear()\n        self.panel.current_shape = None\n        self.panel.selected_shape = None\n        self.panel.Refresh()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Canvas cleared.\")\n\n# --- Main App ---\n\nclass DrawingApp(wx.App):\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    \"\"\"\n    wxPython Shape Drawing Application\n\n    Features:\n    - Draw rectangles, ellipses, and lines by selecting the tool and dragging on the canvas.\n    - Select and move shapes by choosing the selection tool and dragging a shape.\n    - Right-click to deselect.\n    - Toolbar for tool selection and clearing the canvas.\n\n    Integration Notes:\n    - The DrawingPanel class can be embedded in any wxPython application.\n    - Shape classes can be extended for more shapes or features.\n    - All shape logic is encapsulated for easy reuse.\n    \"\"\"\n    app = DrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()",
                        "import wx\n\n# ---- Shape Classes ----\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"Base class for drawable shapes.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, pos, color=wx.BLACK):\n        self.pos = pos  # (x, y)\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape. To be implemented by subclasses.\"\"\"\n        pass\n\n    def contains(self, point):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        pass\n\n    def move(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        self.pos = (self.pos[0] + dx, self.pos[1] + dy)\n\n    def draw_selection(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw selection highlight.\"\"\"\n        if self.selected:\n            pen = wx.Pen(wx.Colour(0, 120, 215), 2, wx.PENSTYLE_DOT)\n            dc.SetPen(pen)\n            dc.SetBrush(wx.TRANSPARENT_BRUSH)\n            bbox = self.get_bbox()\n            dc.DrawRectangle(*bbox)\n\n    def get_bbox(self):\n        \"\"\"Return bounding box (x, y, w, h) for selection highlight.\"\"\"\n        pass\n\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    def __init__(self, pos, size=(80, 60), color=wx.BLUE):\n        super().__init__(pos, color)\n        self.size = size  # (width, height)\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        dc.SetPen(wx.Pen(self.color, 2 if self.selected else 1))\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(self.color if not self.selected else wx.Colour(200, 220, 255)))\n        dc.DrawRectangle(self.pos[0], self.pos[1], self.size[0], self.size[1])\n        self.draw_selection(dc)\n\n    def contains(self, point):\n        x, y = self.pos\n        w, h = self.size\n        px, py = point\n        return x <= px <= x + w and y <= py <= y + h\n\n    def get_bbox(self):\n        return (*self.pos, *self.size)\n\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    def __init__(self, pos, size=(80, 60), color=wx.RED):\n        super().__init__(pos, color)\n        self.size = size\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        dc.SetPen(wx.Pen(self.color, 2 if self.selected else 1))\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(self.color if not self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 220, 220)))\n        dc.DrawEllipse(self.pos[0], self.pos[1], self.size[0], self.size[1])\n        self.draw_selection(dc)\n\n    def contains(self, point):\n        x, y = self.pos\n        w, h = self.size\n        px, py = point\n        # Ellipse equation: ((px-cx)/rx)^2 + ((py-cy)/ry)^2 <= 1\n        cx, cy = x + w/2, y + h/2\n        rx, ry = w/2, h/2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        return ((px - cx) / rx) ** 2 + ((py - cy) / ry) ** 2 <= 1\n\n    def get_bbox(self):\n        return (*self.pos, *self.size)\n\n\nclass TriangleShape(Shape):\n    def __init__(self, pos, size=(80, 60), color=wx.Colour(50, 150, 50)):\n        super().__init__(pos, color)\n        self.size = size\n\n    def get_points(self):\n        x, y = self.pos\n        w, h = self.size\n        # Equilateral triangle pointing up\n        return [\n            (x + w // 2, y),        # Top\n            (x, y + h),             # Bottom left\n            (x + w, y + h)          # Bottom right\n        ]\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        dc.SetPen(wx.Pen(self.color, 2 if self.selected else 1))\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(self.color if not self.selected else wx.Colour(200, 255, 200)))\n        dc.DrawPolygon(self.get_points())\n        self.draw_selection(dc)\n\n    def contains(self, point):\n        # Barycentric technique\n        px, py = point\n        pts = self.get_points()\n        def area(x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3):\n            return abs((x1*(y2-y3) + x2*(y3-y1) + x3*(y1-y2)) / 2.0)\n        A = area(*pts[0], *pts[1], *pts[2])\n        A1 = area(px, py, *pts[1], *pts[2])\n        A2 = area(*pts[0], px, py, *pts[2])\n        A3 = area(*pts[0], *pts[1], px, py)\n        return abs(A - (A1 + A2 + A3)) < 1.0\n\n    def get_bbox(self):\n        x, y = self.pos\n        w, h = self.size\n        return (x, y, w, h)\n\n# ---- Drawing Canvas ----\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"Panel for drawing and interacting with shapes.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.shapes = []  # List of Shape objects\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.dragging = False\n\n        # For drawing new shapes\n        self.drawing = False\n        self.draw_start = None\n        self.draw_shape_type = 'Rectangle'  # Default shape to draw\n\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.WHITE)\n\n        # Bind events\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_shape_type(self, shape_type):\n        \"\"\"Set the type of shape to draw.\"\"\"\n        self.draw_shape_type = shape_type\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        dc = wx.BufferedPaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        # Draw preview of shape while drawing\n        if self.drawing and self.draw_start:\n            x0, y0 = self.draw_start\n            x1, y1 = self.ScreenToClient(wx.GetMousePosition())\n            w, h = x1 - x0, y1 - y0\n            preview_rect = (x0, y0, w, h)\n            pen = wx.Pen(wx.Colour(100, 100, 100), 1, wx.PENSTYLE_DOT)\n            dc.SetPen(pen)\n            dc.SetBrush(wx.TRANSPARENT_BRUSH)\n            if self.draw_shape_type == 'Rectangle':\n                dc.DrawRectangle(*preview_rect)\n            elif self.draw_shape_type == 'Ellipse':\n                dc.DrawEllipse(*preview_rect)\n            elif self.draw_shape_type == 'Triangle':\n                pts = [\n                    (x0 + w // 2, y0),\n                    (x0, y0 + h),\n                    (x0 + w, y0 + h)\n                ]\n                dc.DrawPolygon(pts)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        # Check if clicking on an existing shape (from topmost)\n        for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n            if shape.contains(pos):\n                self.select_shape(shape)\n                self.dragging = True\n                sx, sy = shape.pos\n                self.drag_offset = (pos[0] - sx, pos[1] - sy)\n                self.Refresh()\n                return\n        # Not on a shape: start drawing new shape\n        self.select_shape(None)\n        self.drawing = True\n        self.draw_start = pos\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.drawing and self.draw_start:\n            x0, y0 = self.draw_start\n            x1, y1 = pos\n            w, h = x1 - x0, y1 - y0\n            # Normalize width/height and position\n            if w < 0:\n                x0 += w\n                w = -w\n            if h < 0:\n                y0 += h\n                h = -h\n            if w > 5 and h > 5:  # Ignore tiny shapes\n                if self.draw_shape_type == 'Rectangle':\n                    shape = RectangleShape((x0, y0), (w, h))\n                elif self.draw_shape_type == 'Ellipse':\n                    shape = EllipseShape((x0, y0), (w, h))\n                elif self.draw_shape_type == 'Triangle':\n                    shape = TriangleShape((x0, y0), (w, h))\n                else:\n                    shape = None\n                if shape:\n                    self.shapes.append(shape)\n            self.drawing = False\n            self.draw_start = None\n            self.Refresh()\n        elif self.dragging:\n            self.dragging = False\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.drawing:\n            self.Refresh()  # Update preview\n        elif self.dragging and self.selected_shape and event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            # Move selected shape\n            dx = pos[0] - self.selected_shape.pos[0] - self.drag_offset[0]\n            dy = pos[1] - self.selected_shape.pos[1] - self.drag_offset[1]\n            self.selected_shape.move(dx, dy)\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        # Deselect on right-click\n        self.select_shape(None)\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def select_shape(self, shape):\n        \"\"\"Select a shape and deselect others.\"\"\"\n        for s in self.shapes:\n            s.selected = False\n        if shape:\n            shape.selected = True\n        self.selected_shape = shape\n\n# ---- Main Frame ----\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"Main application window.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"Shape Drawer - wxPython\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n\n        rect_tool = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        ellipse_tool = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        triangle_tool = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Triangle\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Triangle\")\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_shape_type('Rectangle'), rect_tool)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_shape_type('Ellipse'), ellipse_tool)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_shape_type('Triangle'), triangle_tool)\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to select/move shapes, drag to draw. Use toolbar to change shape type. Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n# ---- Application Entry ----\n\nclass ShapeApp(wx.App):\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\"\"\"\nExplanation for Integration:\n\n- The script uses wxPython to create a simple vector drawing app.\n- There are three shape classes: RectangleShape, EllipseShape, and TriangleShape, all derived from a common Shape base.\n- The DrawingPanel handles mouse events for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n- The toolbar at the top lets users choose which shape to draw next.\n- Left-click and drag on empty space to draw a new shape.\n- Left-click on a shape to select and move it (drag).\n- Right-click anywhere to deselect.\n- The code is modular: you can add more shapes by subclassing Shape and updating DrawingPanel.\n- To integrate, use DrawingPanel as a custom widget in your wxPython app and add shape classes as needed.\n\"\"\""

    dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy) if (dx * dx + dy * dy) != 0 else 0\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- Test Suite ---\n\nclass TestShapeDrawing(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    # --- RectangleShape tests ---\n\n    def test_rectangle_contains_inside(self):\n        rect = self.calls.append(('DrawEllipse', x, y, w, h))\n\n    def DrawLine(self, x0, y0, x1, y1):\n        self.calls.append(('DrawLine', x0, y0, x1, y1))\n\nclass MockEvent:\n    def __init__(self, x, y, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        # Compute distance to line segment\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n    super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []  # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None  # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"Set the current tool/mode.\"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Select shape under mouse\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):  # Topmost first\n                if shape.contains(pos):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    # Store offset for dragging\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect others\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def                         "import wx\n\n# --- Shape Classes ---\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"\n    Base class for drawable shapes.\n    Each shape has a start and end point, a selection state, and a color.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start, end, color=wx.BLACK_PEN):\n        self.start = start  # (x, y) tuple\n        self.end = end      # (x, y) tuple\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Rectangle shape. Draws a rectangle between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ellipse shape. Draws an ellipse between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        # Equation of ellipse: ((x-cx)^2)/rx^2 + ((y-cy)^2)/ry^2 <= 1\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Line shape. Draws a line between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- Drawing Panel ---\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Custom panel for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n    Handles all mouse events and shape management.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []  # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None  # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the current tool/mode.\n        mode: 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n        \"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        # Deselect all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Redraw all shapes and the current shape (if any).\"\"\"\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Select shape under mouse (topmost first)\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n                if shape.contains((pos.x, pos.y)):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    # Compute center for drag offset\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect other shapes\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            if self.HasCapture():\n                self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            if self.mode == 'select' and self.selected_shape:\n                # Move selected shape\n                x0, y0 = self.selected_shape.start\n                x1, y1 = self.selected_shape.end\n                cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                dx = pos.x - cx - self.drag_offset[0]\n                dy = pos.y - cy - self.drag_offset[1]\n                self.selected_shape.move_by(dx, dy)\n                self.Refresh()\n            elif self.current_shape:\n                # Update shape endpoint while drawing\n                self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n                self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        # Deselect all shapes on right-click\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n# --- Main Frame ---\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main application window.\n    Contains the DrawingPanel and a toolbar for tool selection.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n        # Use wx.ArtProvider for simple built-in icons\n        self.tool_select = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Select\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Select/Move\")\n        self.tool_rect = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW_DIR, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        self.tool_ellipse = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_TIP, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        self.tool_line = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Line\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Line\")\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events to DrawingPanel mode\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('select'), self.tool_select)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('rectangle'), self.tool_rect)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('ellipse'), self.tool_ellipse)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('line'), self.tool_line)\n\n        # Status bar with instructions\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to draw/select/move. Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n        self.Centre()\n\n# --- Main Application ---\n\nclass ShapeDrawingApp(wx.App):\n    \"\"\"\n    wx.App subclass to start the application.\n    \"\"\"\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeDrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration and Explanation:\n---------------------------\n- This script creates a wxPython GUI application for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes (rectangle, ellipse, line).\n- The DrawingPanel class is a custom wx.Panel that handles all drawing and mouse interaction logic.\n- The toolbar at the top allows users to switch between 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', and 'line' modes.\n- In 'select' mode, left-click on a shape to select it, then drag to move. Right-click anywhere to deselect.\n- In drawing modes, left-click and drag to create a new shape.\n- The Shape base class and its subclasses (RectangleShape, EllipseShape, LineShape) encapsulate drawing and hit-testing logic.\n- To integrate into another wxPython app, use DrawingPanel as a drop-in panel. You can add more shape types by subclassing Shape.\n- Only dependency is wxPython (`pip install wxPython`).\n\"\"\"",
                        "import wx\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Shape Classes\n# ------------------------------\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"Base class for drawable shapes.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start, end, color=wx.BLACK_PEN):\n        self.start = start  # (x, y)\n        self.end = end      # (x, y)\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"Rectangle shape.\"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        brush = wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240))\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(brush)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"Ellipse shape.\"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        brush = wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240))\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(brush)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"Line shape.\"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Drawing Panel\n# ------------------------------\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Custom panel for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []              # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None     # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None    # Currently selected shape\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)     # Offset for dragging\n        self.mode = 'select'          # Current tool/mode\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the current tool/mode ('select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line').\n        \"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        # Deselect all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Paint event handler. Draws all shapes and the shape being drawn.\n        \"\"\"\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Left mouse button down event handler.\n        - In select mode: selects a shape under the cursor.\n        - In draw mode: starts drawing a new shape.\n        \"\"\"\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Try to select the topmost shape under the mouse\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n                if shape.contains((pos.x, pos.y)):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    # Calculate center for drag offset\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect all other shapes\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Left mouse button up event handler.\n        - In select mode: ends dragging.\n        - In draw mode: finishes drawing the new shape.\n        \"\"\"\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape = None\n            if self.HasCapture():\n                self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Mouse move event handler.\n        - In select mode: moves the selected shape if dragging.\n        - In draw mode: updates the shape endpoint.\n        \"\"\"\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            if self.mode == 'select' and self.selected_shape:\n                # Move selected shape\n                x0, y0 = self.selected_shape.start\n                x1, y1 = self.selected_shape.end\n                cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                dx = pos.x - cx - self.drag_offset[0]\n                dy = pos.y - cy - self.drag_offset[1]\n                self.selected_shape.move_by(dx, dy)\n                self.Refresh()\n            elif self.current_shape:\n                # Update shape endpoint while drawing\n                self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n                self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Right mouse button down event handler.\n        Deselects all shapes.\n        \"\"\"\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Main Frame\n# ------------------------------\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main application frame containing the DrawingPanel and toolbar.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n        # Add toolbar tools with standard icons\n        self.tool_select = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Select\",\n                                           wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n                                           shortHelp=\"Select/Move\")\n        self.tool_rect = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\",\n                                         wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW_DIR, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n                                         shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        self.tool_ellipse = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\",\n                                            wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_TIP, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n                                            shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        self.tool_line = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Line\",\n                                         wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n                                         shortHelp=\"Draw Line\")\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events to change mode\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('select'), self.tool_select)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('rectangle'), self.tool_rect)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('ellipse'), self.tool_ellipse)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('line'), self.tool_line)\n\n        # Status bar\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to draw/select/move. Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n        self.Centre()\n\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Main Application\n# ------------------------------\n\nclass ShapeDrawingApp(wx.App):\n    \"\"\"\n    wxPython application class.\n    \"\"\"\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeDrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration/Explanation:\n------------------------\n- The code uses wxPython to create a drawing application with a toolbar for selecting tools (select/move, rectangle, ellipse, line).\n- The DrawingPanel class handles all drawing and mouse interaction logic.\n- Shapes are represented by classes (RectangleShape, EllipseShape, LineShape) inheriting from a base Shape class.\n- Users can:\n    * Draw shapes by selecting a tool and dragging with the left mouse button.\n    * Select and move shapes in 'select' mode by clicking and dragging.\n    * Deselect shapes with a right-click.\n- To integrate into another wxPython app, you can use DrawingPanel as a custom panel, and add/remove shape classes as needed.\n- The code is self-contained and requires only wxPython (`pip install wxPython`).\n\"\"\"",
                        "import wx\n\n# --- Shape Classes ---\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"Base class for drawable shapes.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start, end, color=wx.BLACK_PEN):\n        self.start = start  # (x, y) tuple\n        self.end = end      # (x, y) tuple\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"Rectangle shape implementation.\"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        # Use blue border if selected, otherwise black\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        # Use a different fill color if selected\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"Ellipse shape implementation.\"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        # Check if point is inside the ellipse using the standard ellipse equation\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"Line shape implementation.\"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto the line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n\n# --- Drawing Panel ---\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Panel that handles drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []  # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None  # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the current tool/mode.\n        \"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        # Deselect all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Handle the paint event: draw all shapes and the current shape (if any).\n        \"\"\"\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Handle left mouse button down event.\n        - In 'select' mode: select a shape.\n        - In drawing mode: start drawing a new shape.\n        \"\"\"\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Try to select the topmost shape under the mouse\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):  # Topmost first\n                if shape.contains((pos.x, pos.y)):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    # Compute center for drag offset\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect all others\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Handle left mouse button up event.\n        - In drawing mode: finish drawing the shape and add it to the list.\n        \"\"\"\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            if self.HasCapture():\n                self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Handle mouse move event.\n        - In 'select' mode: drag the selected shape.\n        - In drawing mode: update the endpoint of the current shape.\n        \"\"\"\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            if self.mode == 'select' and self.selected_shape:\n                # Move selected shape\n                x0, y0 = self.selected_shape.start\n                x1, y1 = self.selected_shape.end\n                cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                dx = pos.x - cx - self.drag_offset[0]\n                dy = pos.y - cy - self.drag_offset[1]\n                self.selected_shape.move_by(dx, dy)\n                self.Refresh()\n            elif self.current_shape:\n                # Update shape endpoint while drawing\n                self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n                self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        \"\"\"\n        Handle right mouse button down event.\n        - Deselect all shapes.\n        \"\"\"\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n\n# --- Main Frame ---\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main application frame with toolbar and drawing panel.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n        self.tool_select = toolbar.AddTool(\n            wx.ID_ANY, \"Select\",\n            wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n            shortHelp=\"Select/Move\"\n        )\n        self.tool_rect = toolbar.AddTool(\n            wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\",\n            wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW_DIR, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n            shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\"\n        )\n        self.tool_ellipse = toolbar.AddTool(\n            wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\",\n            wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_TIP, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n            shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\"\n        )\n        self.tool_line = toolbar.AddTool(\n            wx.ID_ANY, \"Line\",\n            wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)),\n            shortHelp=\"Draw Line\"\n        )\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events to change the drawing mode\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('select'), self.tool_select)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('rectangle'), self.tool_rect)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('ellipse'), self.tool_ellipse)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('line'), self.tool_line)\n\n        # Status bar\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to draw/select/move. dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK_PEN, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK_PEN, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7\n\n# --- Test Suite ---\n\nclass TestShapeClasses(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    # --- RectangleShape Tests ---\n\n    def test_rectangle_contains_inside_and_outside(self):\n                     "best_code": "import wx\n\n# --- Shape Classes ---\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"\n    Base class for drawable shapes.\n    Each shape has a start and end point, a selection state, and a color.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start, end, color=wx.BLACK_PEN):\n        self.start = start  # (x, y) tuple\n        self.end = end      # (x, y) tuple\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Rectangle shape. Draws a rectangle between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ellipse shape. Draws an ellipse between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        # Equation of ellipse: ((x-cx)^2)/rx^2 + ((y-cy)^2)/ry^2 <= 1\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Line shape. Draws a line between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- Drawing Panel ---\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Custom panel for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n    Handles all mouse events and shape management.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []  # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None  # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the current tool/mode.\n        mode: 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n        \"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        # Deselect all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Redraw all shapes and the current shape (if any).\"\"\"\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Select shape under mouse (topmost first)\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n                if shape.contains((pos.x, pos.y)):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    # Compute center for drag offset\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect other shapes\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            if self.HasCapture():\n                self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            if self.mode == 'select' and self.selected_shape:\n                # Move selected shape\n                x0, y0 = self.selected_shape.start\n                x1, y1 = self.selected_shape.end\n                cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                dx = pos.x - cx - self.drag_offset[0]\n                dy = pos.y - cy - self.drag_offset[1]\n                self.selected_shape.move_by(dx, dy)\n                self.Refresh()\n            elif self.current_shape:\n                # Update shape endpoint while drawing\n                self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n                self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        # Deselect all shapes on right-click\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n# --- Main Frame ---\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main application window.\n    Contains the DrawingPanel and a toolbar for tool selection.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n        # Use wx.ArtProvider for simple built-in icons\n        self.tool_select = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Select\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Select/Move\")\n        self.tool_rect = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW_DIR, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        self.tool_ellipse = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_TIP, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        self.tool_line = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Line\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Line\")\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events to DrawingPanel mode\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('select'), self.tool_select)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('rectangle'), self.tool_rect)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('ellipse'), self.tool_ellipse)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('line'), self.tool_line)\n\n        # Status bar with instructions\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to draw/select/move. Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n        self.Centre()\n\n# --- Main Application ---\n\nclass ShapeDrawingApp(wx.App):\n    \"\"\"\n    wx.App subclass to start the application.\n    \"\"\"\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeDrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration and Explanation:\n---------------------------\n- This script creates a wxPython GUI application for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes (rectangle, ellipse, line).\n- The DrawingPanel class is a custom wx.Panel that handles all drawing and mouse interaction logic.\n- The toolbar at the top allows users to switch between 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', and 'line' modes.\n- In 'select' mode, left-click on a shape to select it, then drag to move.
