                        "import wx\n\n# --- Shape Classes ---\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"\n    Base class for drawable shapes.\n    Each shape has a start and end point, a selection state, and a color.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start, end, color=wx.BLACK_PEN):\n        self.start = start  # (x, y) tuple\n        self.end = end      # (x, y) tuple\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Rectangle shape. Draws a rectangle between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ellipse shape. Draws an ellipse between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        # Equation of ellipse: ((x-cx)^2)/rx^2 + ((y-cy)^2)/ry^2 <= 1\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Line shape. Draws a line between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- Drawing Panel ---\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Custom panel for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n    Handles all mouse events and shape management.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []  # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None  # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the current tool/mode.\n        mode: 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n        \"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        # Deselect all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Redraw all shapes and the current shape (if any).\"\"\"\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Select shape under mouse (topmost first)\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n                if shape.contains((pos.x, pos.y)):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    # Compute center for drag offset\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect other shapes\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            if self.HasCapture():\n                self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            if self.mode == 'select' and self.selected_shape:\n                # Move selected shape\n                x0, y0 = self.selected_shape.start\n                x1, y1 = self.selected_shape.end\n                cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                dx = pos.x - cx - self.drag_offset[0]\n                dy = pos.y - cy - self.drag_offset[1]\n                self.selected_shape.move_by(dx, dy)\n                self.Refresh()\n            elif self.current_shape:\n                # Update shape endpoint while drawing\n                self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n                self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        # Deselect all shapes on right-click\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n# --- Main Frame ---\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main application window.\n    Contains the DrawingPanel and a toolbar for tool selection.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n        # Use wx.ArtProvider for simple built-in icons\n        self.tool_select = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Select\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Select/Move\")\n        self.tool_rect = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW_DIR, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        self.tool_ellipse = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_TIP, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        self.tool_line = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Line\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Line\")\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events to DrawingPanel mode\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('select'), self.tool_select)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('rectangle'), self.tool_rect)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('ellipse'), self.tool_ellipse)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('line'), self.tool_line)\n\n        # Status bar with instructions\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to draw/select/move. Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n        self.Centre()\n\n# --- Main Application ---\n\nclass ShapeDrawingApp(wx.App):\n    \"\"\"\n    wx.App subclass to start the application.\n    \"\"\"\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeDrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration and Explanation:\n---------------------------\n- This script creates a wxPython GUI application for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes (rectangle, ellipse, line).\n- The DrawingPanel class is a custom wx.Panel that handles all drawing and mouse interaction logic.\n- The toolbar at the top allows users to switch between 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', and 'line' modes.\n- In 'select' mode, left-click on a shape to select it, then drag to move. Right-click anywhere to deselect.\n- In drawing modes, left-click and drag to create a new shape.\n- The Shape base class and its subclasses (RectangleShape, EllipseShape, LineShape) encapsulate drawing and hit-testing logic.\n- To integrate into another wxPython app, use DrawingPanel as a drop-in panel. You can add more shape types by subclassing Shape.\n- Only dependency is wxPython (`pip install wxPython`).\n\"\"\"",

Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n        self.Centre()\n\n# --- Main Application ---\n\nclass ShapeDrawingApp(wx.App):\n    \"\"\"\n    wx.App subclass to start the application.\n    \"\"\"\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeDrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration and Explanation:\n---------------------------\n- This script creates a wxPython GUI application for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes (rectangle, ellipse, line).\n- The DrawingPanel class is a custom wx.Panel that handles all drawing and mouse interaction logic.\n- The toolbar at the top allows users to switch between 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', and 'line' modes.\n- In 'select' mode, left-click on a shape to select it, then drag to move. Right-click anywhere to deselect.\n- In drawing modes, left-click and drag to create a new shape.\n- The Shape base class and its subclasses (RectangleShape, EllipseShape, LineShape) encapsulate drawing and hit-testing logic.\n- To integrate into another wxPython app, use DrawingPanel as a drop-in panel. You can add more shape types by subclassing Shape.\n- Only dependency is wxPython (`pip install wxPython`).\n\"\"\"",
                        "import wx\n\n# --- Shape Classes ---\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"\n    Abstract base class for drawable shapes.\n    Each shape has a start and end point, a selection state, and a color.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start, end, color=wx.BLACK_PEN):\n        self.start = start  # (x, y) tuple\n        self.end = end      # (x, y) tuple\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Rectangle shape. Draws a rectangle between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ellipse shape. Draws an ellipse between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        # Equation of ellipse: ((x-cx)^2)/rx^2 + ((y-cy)^2)/ry^2 <= 1\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Line shape. Draws a line between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- Drawing Panel ---\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Custom panel for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n    Handles all mouse events and shape management.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []  # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None  # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the current tool/mode.\n        mode: 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n        \"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        # Deselect all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Redraw all shapes and the current shape (if any).\"\"\"\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Select shape under mouse (topmost first)\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n                if shape.contains((pos.x, pos.y)):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    # Compute center for drag offset\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect other shapes\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            if self.HasCapture():\n                self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            if self.mode == 'select' and self.selected_shape:\n                # Move selected shape\n                x0, y0 = self.selected_shape.start\n                x1, y1 = self.selected_shape.end\n                cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                dx = pos.x - cx - self.drag_offset[0]\n                dy = pos.y - cy - self.drag_offset[1]\n                self.selected_shape.move_by(dx, dy)\n                self.Refresh()\n            elif self.current_shape:\n                # Update shape endpoint while drawing\n                self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n                self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        # Deselect all shapes on right-click\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n# --- Main Frame ---\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main application window.\n    Contains the DrawingPanel and a toolbar for tool selection.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n        # Use wx.ArtProvider for simple built-in icons\n        self.tool_select = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Select\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Select/Move\")\n        self.tool_rect = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW_DIR, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        self.tool_ellipse = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_TIP, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        self.tool_line = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Line\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Line\")\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events to DrawingPanel mode\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('select'), self.tool_select)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('rectangle'), self.tool_rect)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('ellipse'), self.tool_ellipse)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('line'), self.tool_line)\n\n        # Status bar with instructions\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to draw/select/move. Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n        self.Centre()\n\n# --- Main Application ---\n\nclass ShapeDrawingApp(wx.App):\n    \"\"\"\n    wx.App subclass to start the application.\n    \"\"\"\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeDrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration and Explanation:\n---------------------------\n- This script creates a wxPython GUI application for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes (rectangle, ellipse, line).\n- The DrawingPanel class is a custom wx.Panel that handles all drawing and mouse interaction logic.\n- The toolbar at the top allows users to switch between 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', and 'line' modes.\n- In 'select' mode, left-click on a shape to select it, then drag to move. Right-click anywhere to deselect.\n- In drawing modes, left-click and drag to create a new shape.\n- The Shape base class and its subclasses (RectangleShape, EllipseShape, LineShape) encapsulate drawing and hit-testing logic.\n- To integrate into another wxPython app, use DrawingPanel as a drop-in panel.                         "import unittest\n\n# Since the code to test depends on wxPython and GUI elements, we focus on the logic of the Shape classes.\n# We'll mock wx.Pen, wx.Brush, wx.Colour, and the device context for draw methods, and test the logic for contains and move_by.\n\nimport sys\n\ntry:\n    import wx\nexcept ImportError:\n    # (x, y) tuple\n        self.end = end      # (x, y) tuple\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Rectangle shape. Draws a rectangle between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ellipse shape. Draws an ellipse between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        # Equation of ellipse: ((x-cx)^2)/rx^2 + ((y-cy)^2)/ry^2 <= 1\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Line shape. Draws a line between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- Tests ---\n\nclass TestShapeBase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_move_by(self):\n        s = Shape((1, 2), (3, 4))\n        s.move_by(10, -2)\n        self.assertEqual(s.start, (11, 0))\n        self.assertEqual(s.end, (13, 2))\n\n    def test_draw_not_implemented(self):\n        s = Shape((0, 0), (1, 1))\n        with self.assertRaises(NotImplementedError):\n            s.draw(None)\n\n    def test_contains_not_implemented(self):\n        s = Shape((0, 0), (1, 1))\n        with self.assertRaises(NotImplementedError):\n            s.contains((0, 0))\n\nclass TestRectangleShape(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Degenerate ellipse (line)\n        ellipse = EllipseShape((10, 20), (10, 40))\n        self.assertFalse(ellipse.contains((10, 30)))\n        self.assertFalse(ellipse.contains((10, 20)))\n        self.assertFalse(ellipse.contains((10, 40)))\n\n    def test_zero_height(self):\n        ellipse = EllipseShape((10, 20), (30, 20))\n        self.assertFalse(ellipse.contains((20, 20)))\n\n    def test_negative_size(self):\n        #    x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n EllipseShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7\n\n# --- Test Suite ---\n\nclass TestShapeBase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def test_move_by(self):\n        s = Shape((1, 2), (3, 4))\n Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- Drawing Panel ---\n\nclass DrawingPanel(wx.Panel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Custom panel for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes.\n    Handles all mouse events and shape management.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, parent):\n        super().__init__(parent)\n        self.SetBackgroundColour(wx.Colour(255, 255, 255))\n        self.shapes = []  # List of all shapes\n        self.current_shape = None  # Shape being drawn\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        self.mode = 'select'  # 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n\n        # Mouse event bindings\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_PAINT, self.on_paint)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_DOWN, self.on_left_down)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_LEFT_UP, self.on_left_up)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_MOTION, self.on_mouse_move)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_RIGHT_DOWN, self.on_right_down)\n\n    def set_mode(self, mode):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the current tool/mode.\n        mode: 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', 'line'\n        \"\"\"\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.current_shape = None\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        # Deselect all shapes\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_paint(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Redraw all shapes and the current shape (if any).\"\"\"\n        dc = wx.PaintDC(self)\n        dc.Clear()\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.draw(dc)\n        if self.current_shape:\n            self.current_shape.draw(dc)\n\n    def on_left_down(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            # Select shape under mouse (topmost first)\n            self.selected_shape = None\n            for shape in reversed(self.shapes):\n                if shape.contains((pos.x, pos.y)):\n                    self.selected_shape = shape\n                    shape.selected = True\n                    # Compute center for drag offset\n                    x0, y0 = shape.start\n                    x1, y1 = shape.end\n                    cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                    cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                    self.drag_offset = (pos.x - cx, pos.y - cy)\n                    break\n            # Deselect other shapes\n            for shape in self.shapes:\n                if shape != self.selected_shape:\n                    shape.selected = False\n            self.Refresh()\n        else:\n            # Start drawing a new shape\n            if self.mode == 'rectangle':\n                self.current_shape = RectangleShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'ellipse':\n                self.current_shape = EllipseShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            elif self.mode == 'line':\n                self.current_shape = LineShape((pos.x, pos.y), (pos.x, pos.y))\n            self.CaptureMouse()\n\n    def on_left_up(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if self.mode == 'select':\n            self.drag_offset = (0, 0)\n        elif self.current_shape:\n            # Finish drawing shape\n            self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n            self.shapes.append(self.current_shape)\n            self.current_shape.selected = False\n            self.current_shape = None\n            if self.HasCapture():\n                self.ReleaseMouse()\n            self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_mouse_move(self, event):\n        pos = event.GetPosition()\n        if event.Dragging() and event.LeftIsDown():\n            if self.mode == 'select' and self.selected_shape:\n                # Move selected shape\n                x0, y0 = self.selected_shape.start\n                x1, y1 = self.selected_shape.end\n                cx = (x0 + x1) // 2\n                cy = (y0 + y1) // 2\n                dx = pos.x - cx - self.drag_offset[0]\n                dy = pos.y - cy - self.drag_offset[1]\n                self.selected_shape.move_by(dx, dy)\n                self.Refresh()\n            elif self.current_shape:\n                # Update shape endpoint while drawing\n                self.current_shape.end = (pos.x, pos.y)\n                self.Refresh()\n\n    def on_right_down(self, event):\n        # Deselect all shapes on right-click\n        for shape in self.shapes:\n            shape.selected = False\n        self.selected_shape = None\n        self.Refresh()\n\n# --- Main Frame ---\n\nclass MainFrame(wx.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main application window.\n    Contains the DrawingPanel and a toolbar for tool selection.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__(None, title=\"wxPython Shape Drawing\", size=(800, 600))\n        self.panel = DrawingPanel(self)\n\n        # Toolbar for shape selection\n        toolbar = wx.ToolBar(self)\n        self.SetToolBar(toolbar)\n        # Use wx.ArtProvider for simple built-in icons\n        self.tool_select = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Select\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NORMAL_FILE, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Select/Move\")\n        self.tool_rect = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Rectangle\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_NEW_DIR, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Rectangle\")\n        self.tool_ellipse = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Ellipse\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_TIP, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Ellipse\")\n        self.tool_line = toolbar.AddTool(wx.ID_ANY, \"Line\", wx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap(wx.ART_MINUS, wx.ART_TOOLBAR, (16,16)), shortHelp=\"Draw Line\")\n        toolbar.Realize()\n\n        # Bind toolbar events to DrawingPanel mode\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('select'), self.tool_select)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('rectangle'), self.tool_rect)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('ellipse'), self.tool_ellipse)\n        self.Bind(wx.EVT_TOOL, lambda evt: self.panel.set_mode('line'), self.tool_line)\n\n        # Status bar with instructions\n        self.CreateStatusBar()\n        self.SetStatusText(\"Left-click to draw/select/move. Right-click to deselect.\")\n\n        # Layout\n        sizer = wx.BoxSizer(wx.VERTICAL)\n        sizer.Add(self.panel, 1, wx.EXPAND)\n        self.SetSizer(sizer)\n        self.Centre()\n\n# --- Main Application ---\n\nclass ShapeDrawingApp(wx.App):\n    \"\"\"\n    wx.App subclass to start the application.\n    \"\"\"\n    def OnInit(self):\n        frame = MainFrame()\n        frame.Show()\n        return True\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app = ShapeDrawingApp(False)\n    app.MainLoop()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration and Explanation:\n---------------------------\n- This script creates a wxPython GUI application for drawing, selecting, and moving shapes (rectangle, ellipse, line).\n- The DrawingPanel class is a custom wx.Panel that handles all drawing and mouse interaction logic.\n- The toolbar at the top allows users to switch between 'select', 'rectangle', 'ellipse', and 'line' modes.\n- In 'select' mode, left-click on a shape to select it, then drag to move. Right-click anywhere to deselect.\n- In drawing modes, left-click and drag to create a new shape.\n- The Shape base class and its subclasses (RectangleShape, EllipseShape, LineShape) encapsulate drawing and hit-testing logic.\n- To integrate into another wxPython app, use DrawingPanel as a drop-in panel. You can add more shape types by subclassing Shape.\n- Only dependency is wxPython (`pip install wxPython`).\n\"\"\"",
                    "best_tests": "import unittest\n\n# Since the code to test uses wxPython and GUI, we focus on testing the logic of the Shape classes.\n# We do NOT test GUI events or wx.Panel, but we do test RectangleShape, EllipseShape, and LineShape.\n\n# Minimal stubs for wx classes used in Shape constructors (for headless testing)\nclass DummyPen:\n    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs): pass\n\nclass DummyBrush:\n    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs): pass\n\nclass DummyColour:\n    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs): pass\n\nclass DummyDC:\n    def SetPen(self, pen): pass\n    def SetBrush(self, brush): pass\n    def DrawRectangle(self, x, y, w, h): pass\n    def DrawEllipse(self, x, y, w, h): pass\n    def DrawLine(self, x0, y0, x1, y1): pass\n    def Clear(self): pass\n\nclass DummyEvent:\n    def __init__(self, x, y, dragging=False, left_down=False):\n        self._pos = DummyPoint(x, y)\n        self._dragging = dragging\n        self._left_down = left_down\n    def GetPosition(self):\n        return self._pos\n    def Dragging(self):\n        return self._dragging\n    def LeftIsDown(self):\n        return self._left_down\n\nclass DummyPoint:\n    def __init__(self, x, y):\n        self.x = x\n        self.y = y\n\n# Patch wx module for shape classes\nimport sys\nimport types\n\nwx = types.SimpleNamespace()\nwx.Pen = DummyPen\nwx.Brush = DummyBrush\nwx.Colour = DummyColour\nwx.BLACK_PEN = 'BLACK'\nwx.BLUE = 'BLUE'\nwx.RED = 'RED'\nwx.GREEN = 'GREEN'\nwx.BLACK = 'BLACK'\nwx.ArtProvider = types.SimpleNamespace()\nwx.ArtProvider.GetBitmap = lambda *a, **k: None\nwx.ART_NORMAL_FILE = wx.ART_NEW_DIR = wx.ART_TIP = wx.ART_MINUS = wx.ART_TOOLBAR = 0\n\nsys.modules['wx'] = wx\n\n# --- Copy the Shape classes here for testing ---\n\nclass Shape:\n    \"\"\"\n    Base class for drawable shapes.\n    Each shape has a start and end point, a selection state, and a color.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, start, end, color=wx.BLACK_PEN):\n        self.start = start  # (x, y) tuple\n        self.end = end      # (x, y) tuple\n        self.selected = False\n        self.color = color\n\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        \"\"\"Draw the shape using the given device context.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        \"\"\"Check if a point (x, y) is inside the shape.\"\"\"\n        raise NotImplementedError\n\n    def move_by(self, dx, dy):\n        \"\"\"Move the shape by (dx, dy).\"\"\"\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        self.start = (x0 + dx, y0 + dy)\n        self.end = (x1 + dx, y1 + dy)\n\nclass RectangleShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Rectangle shape. Draws a rectangle between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.BLUE if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(200, 200, 255) if self.selected else wx.Colour(240, 240, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawRectangle(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        left = min(x0, x1)\n        right = max(x0, x1)\n        top = min(y0, y1)\n        bottom = max(y0, y1)\n        x, y = pt\n        return left <= x <= right and top <= y <= bottom\n\nclass EllipseShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ellipse shape. Draws an ellipse between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.RED if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.SetBrush(wx.Brush(wx.Colour(255, 220, 220) if self.selected else wx.Colour(255, 255, 240)))\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        dc.DrawEllipse(min(x0, x1), min(y0, y1), abs(x1 - x0), abs(y1 - y0))\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        rx = abs(x1 - x0) / 2\n        ry = abs(y1 - y0) / 2\n        if rx == 0 or ry == 0:\n            return False\n        cx = min(x0, x1) + rx\n        cy = min(y0, y1) + ry\n        x, y = pt\n        # Equation of ellipse: ((x-cx)^2)/rx^2 + ((y-cy)^2)/ry^2 <= 1\n        return ((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1\n\nclass LineShape(Shape):\n    \"\"\"\n    Line shape. Draws a line between start and end points.\n    \"\"\"\n    def draw(self, dc):\n        pen = wx.Pen(wx.GREEN if self.selected else wx.BLACK, width=2)\n        dc.SetPen(pen)\n        dc.DrawLine(self.start[0], self.start[1], self.end[0], self.end[1])\n\n    def contains(self, pt):\n        # Check if point is near the line segment (within a threshold)\n        x0, y0 = self.start\n        x1, y1 = self.end\n        px, py = pt\n        dx = x1 - x0\n        dy = y1 - y0\n        if dx == dy == 0:\n            # Line is a point\n            return abs(px - x0) < 5 and abs(py - y0) < 5\n        # Project point onto line, clamp to segment\n        t = ((px - x0) * dx + (py - y0) * dy) / float(dx * dx + dy * dy)\n        t = max(0, min(1, t))\n        lx = x0 + t * dx\n        ly = y0 + t * dy\n        dist = ((px - lx) ** 2 + (py - ly) ** 2) ** 0.5\n        return dist < 7  # threshold for selection\n\n# --- TEST SUITE ---\n\nclass TestShapeClasses(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def test_rectangle_contains_inside_and_outside(self):\n        rect = RectangleShape((10, 10), (50, 50))\n        self.assertTrue(rect.contains((30, 30)))\n        self.assertTrue(rect.contains((10, 10)))\n        self.assertTrue(rect.contains((50, 50)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((9, 10)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((10, 9)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((51, 50)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((50, 51)))\n\n    def test_rectangle_contains_negative_coordinates(self):\n        rect = RectangleShape((50, 50), (10, 10))\n        self.assertTrue(rect.contains((30, 30)))\n        self.assertTrue(rect.contains((10, 10)))\n        self.assertTrue(rect.contains((50, 50)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((9, 10)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((10, 9)))\n\n    def test_rectangle_zero_area(self):\n        rect = RectangleShape((20, 20), (20, 20))\n        self.assertTrue(rect.contains((20, 20)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((21, 20)))\n        self.assertFalse(rect.contains((20, 21)))\n\n    def test_rectangle_move_by(self):\n        rect = RectangleShape((10, 10), (20, 20))\n        rect.move_by(5, -5)\n        self.assertEqual(rect.start, (15, 5))\n        self.assertEqual(rect.end, (25, 15))\n\n    def test_ellipse_contains_inside_and_outside(self):\n        ell = EllipseShape((10, 10), (50, 50))\n        self.assertTrue(ell.contains((30, 30)))\n        self.assertTrue(ell.contains((10, 30)))\n        self.assertTrue(ell.contains((50, 30)))\n        self.assertFalse(ell.contains((10, 10)))  # On the edge\n        self.assertFalse(ell.contains((5, 5)))\n        self.assertFalse(ell.contains((30, 5)))\n        self.assertFalse(ell.contains((30, 55)))\n\n    def test_ellipse_contains_zero_area(self):\n        ell = EllipseShape((20, 20), (20, 20))\n        self.assertFalse(ell.contains((20, 20)))\n        self.assertFalse(ell.contains((21, 20)))\n\n    def test_ellipse_move_by(self):\n        ell = EllipseShape((10, 10), (20, 30))\n        ell.move_by(-5, 10)\n        self.assertEqual(ell.start, (5, 20))\n        self.assertEqual(ell.end, (15, 40))\n\n    def test_line_contains_on_line_and_near(self):\n        line = LineShape((10, 10), (50, 10))\n        # On the line\n        self.assertTrue(line.contains((30, 10)))\n        # Near the line (within threshold)\n        self.assertTrue(line.contains((30, 13)))\n        # Far from the line\n        self.assertFalse(line.contains((30, 20)))\n\n    def test_line_contains_vertical(self):\n        line = LineShape((20, 10), (20, 50))\n        self.assertTrue(line.contains((20, 30)))\n        self.assertTrue(line.contains((23, 30)))\n        self.assertFalse(line.contains((30, 30)))\n\n    def test_line_contains_point_line(self):\n        line = LineShape((10, 10), (10, 10))\n        self.assertTrue(line.contains((10, 10)))\n        self.assertTrue(line.contains((12, 10)))\n        self.assertFalse(line.contains((16, 10)))\n\n    def test_line_move_by(self):\n        line = LineShape((10, 10), (20, 20))\n        line.move_by(5, -5)\n        self.assertEqual(line.start, (15, 5))\n        self.assertEqual(line.end, (25, 15))\n\n    def test_draw_methods_do_not_raise(self):\n        #
